`pkg/services/ngalert/store/compat.go`: Conversion functions between the internal `alertRule` DB model and the `models.AlertRule` domain model (`alertRuleToModelsAlertRule`, `alertRuleFromModelsAlertRule`).\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/instance_database.go`: Stores alert instance state.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/models.go`: Internal DB model structs for alert rules and instances.\\n\\n3. **Legacy storage (SQL-backed adapter for Kubernetes-style API)** – in the current codebase, 'legacy storage' refers to the SQL-backed implementations used by the Grafana Kubernetes API server as opposed to a future etcd-backed unified storage:\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for alerting rules exposed via the K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/storage.go`: Factory that creates the `legacyStorage` instance.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for recording rules via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/storage.go`: Factory for recording rule legacy storage.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/receiver/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for notification receivers via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/routingtree/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for routing tree via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/templategroup/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for template groups via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/timeinterval/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for time intervals via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/config.go`: Alertmanager config store backed by SQL (`alertmanagerConfigStoreImpl`).\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/persist.go`: Defines `AMConfigStore` interface for alertmanager config access.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/receivers.go`: Receiver data access via SQL.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/compat.go`: Compatibility/conversion functions between internal models and API models.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/errors.go`: Error types for the legacy storage.\\n\\n4. **Migration scripts** – convert legacy (dashboard-based) alerting to unified alerting:\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go`: Defines the original legacy alerting SQL schema (tables: `alert`, `alert_rule_tag`, `alert_notification`, `alert_notification_state`).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go`: Creates all unified alerting SQL tables (`alert_definition`, `alert_rule`, `alert_rule_version`, `alert_instance`, `alert_configuration`, etc.).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/migration_service_migration.go`: Moves the legacy alerting migration status from the migration log table to the kvstore (`MigrationServiceMigration`).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/org_upgrade_state_mig.go`: Manages org-level upgrade state between Legacy and UnifiedAlerting modes (`CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries`).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/created_folders_mig.go`: Migration for tracking folders created during legacy alerting migration.\\n\\nNote: In Grafana 11+, the classic (dashboard panel-based) legacy alerting engine was completely removed. `pkg/services/ngalert/store/compat.go`: Conversion functions between the internal `alertRule` DB model and the `models.AlertRule` domain model (`alertRuleToModelsAlertRule`, `alertRuleFromModelsAlertRule`).\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/instance_database.go`: Stores alert instance state.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/models.go`: Internal DB model structs for alert rules and instances.\\n\\n3. **Legacy storage (SQL-backed adapter for Kubernetes-style API)** – in the current codebase, 'legacy storage' refers to the SQL-backed implementations used by the Grafana Kubernetes API server as opposed to a future etcd-backed unified storage:\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for alerting rules exposed via the K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/storage.go`: Factory that creates the `legacyStorage` instance.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for recording rules via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/storage.go`: Factory for recording rule legacy storage.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/receiver/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for notification receivers via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/routingtree/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for routing tree via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/templategroup/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for template groups via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/timeinterval/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for time intervals via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/config.go`: Alertmanager config store backed by SQL (`alertmanagerConfigStoreImpl`).\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/persist.go`: Defines `AMConfigStore` interface for alertmanager config access.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/receivers.go`: Receiver data access via SQL.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/compat.go`: Compatibility/conversion functions between internal models and API models.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/errors.go`: Error types for the legacy storage.\\n\\n4. **Migration scripts** – convert legacy (dashboard-based) alerting to unified alerting:\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go`: Defines the original legacy alerting SQL schema (tables: `alert`, `alert_rule_tag`, `alert_notification`, `alert_notification_state`).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/ualert.go`: Main migration logic (`upgradeNgAlerting`) that moves pre-8.2 alertmanager configs to per-org directories, and `FixEarlyMigration` / `updateDashboardUIDPanelIDMigration` functions for migrating dashboard alert annotation data into unified alerting.\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go`: Creates all unified alerting SQL tables (`alert_definition`, `alert_rule`, `alert_rule_version`, `alert_instance`, `alert_configuration`, etc.).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/migration_service_migration.go`: Moves the legacy alerting migration status from the migration log table to the kvstore (`MigrationServiceMigration`).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/org_upgrade_state_mig.go`: Manages org-level upgrade state between Legacy and UnifiedAlerting modes (`CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries`).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/alert_rule_state_table.go`: Adds the alert_rule_state table as part of the migration.\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/rule_group_index_migration.go`: Adds rule_group_index column to alert rules.\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/created_folders_mig.go`: Migration for tracking folders created during legacy alerting migration.\\n\\nNote: In Grafana 11+, the classic (dashboard panel-based) legacy alerting engine was completely removed. The 'legacy' terminology in the current codebase refers to the SQL-backed adapter layer for the Kubernetes-style API server (as opposed to future etcd-based unified storage), while ngalert IS the unified alerting engine.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
